contains a comprehensive migration system to convert legacy alerting rules to unified alerting (ngalert). The system is organized in three main components:\\n\\n## Legacy Alerting Engine\\nThe legacy alerting system is defined in `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/alert_mig.go` (github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec), which contains the database schema for the old alert table structure. Legacy alerting has been removed in Grafana v11, as evidenced by the checks in `pkg/setting/setting.go` that prevent enabling legacy alerting.\\n\\n## Unified Alerting (ngalert) Engine\\nThe unified alerting engine is implemented in `pkg/services/ngalert/` with the following key components:\\n\\n1. **Data Models** (`pkg/services/ngalert/models/alert_rule.go`): Defines the `AlertRule` struct for unified alerting with properties like ID, GUID, OrgID, Title, Condition, Data, UID, NamespaceUID, RuleGroup, NoDataState, and ExecErrState.\\n\\n2. **Storage Layer** (`pkg/services/ngalert/store/`): \\n   - `alert_rule.go`: Implements alert rule persistence\\n   - `alertmanager.go`: Manages alertmanager configurations\\n   - `database.go`: Database abstraction layer\\n   - These files implement the DBstore interface for unified alert rule storage\\n\\n3. **Main Service** (`pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go`): The AlertNG service orchestrates all alerting components including metrics, API handlers, scheduler, notifier, and provisioning services.\\n\\n4. **Provisioning** (`pkg/services/ngalert/provisioning/`): \\n   - `alert_rules.go`: AlertRuleService with CreateAlertRule, UpdateAlertRule, DeleteAlertRule methods\\n   - `persist.go`: Persistence interface definitions\\n   - `compat.go`: Compatibility layer for converting between formats\\n\\n5. **Notifier** (`pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/`):\\n   - `receiver_svc.go`: Receiver service for managing notification channels\\n   - `crypto.go`: Encryption/decryption for sensitive configuration\\n   - `legacy_storage/`: Handles legacy alertmanager configuration compatibility\\n\\n## Migration System\\nThe migration from legacy to unified alerting is implemented in `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/` with multiple migration files:\\n\\n1. **ualert.go**: Core migration entry point containing:\\n   - `FixEarlyMigration()`: Fixes organizations and alertmanager configuration files created before v8.2\\n   - `upgradeNgAlerting`: Migration struct that handles organization ID assignments\\n   - `updateAlertmanagerFiles()`: Moves alertmanager configuration files to organization-specific directories\\n\\n2. **tables.go**: Defines database schema migrations:\\n   - `AddTablesMigrations()`: Creates alert_rule, alert_rule_version, alert_instance, alert_configuration tables\\n   - `addAlertRuleMigrations()`: Creates the alert_rule table with columns for org_id, title, condition, data, interval_seconds, namespace_uid, rule_group\\n   - `addAlertmanagerConfigMigrations()`: Creates alert_configuration table for storing alertmanager configurations\\n   - Includes index creation and column modifications for schema evolution\\n\\n3. **org_upgrade_state_mig.go**: Tracks alerting type per organization (Legacy vs UnifiedAlerting)\\n\\n4. **created_folders_mig.go**: Migrates records of folders created during the legacy alert migration process\\n\\n5. **migration_service_migration.go**: Moves legacy alert migration status from migration log to kvstore with namespace \\\"ngalert.migration\\\"\\n\\n6. **accesscontrol/alerting.go**: Migrates alerting-related permissions and action names\\n\\n## Legacy Storage Bridges\\nMultiple legacy storage implementations provide compatibility between old and new systems:\\n\\n1. **Alertmanager Configuration**: `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/config.go` implements `alertmanagerConfigStoreImpl` for reading/writing legacy Alertmanager configurations\\n\\n2. **Receiver Management**: `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/` contains:\\n   - `receivers.go`: Manages receiver CRUD operations with conversion functions\\n   - `compat.go`: Implements `ReceiverToPostableApiReceiver()` and `PostableApiReceiverToReceiver()` for format conversion\\n   - `errors.go`: Error definitions for receiver operations\\n\\n3. **REST API Bridges**:\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/alertrule/legacy_storage.go`: Legacy REST API storage for alert rules\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/recordingrule/legacy_storage.go`: Legacy storage for recording rules\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/receiver/legacy_storage.go`: Legacy storage for receivers\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/routingtree/legacy_storage.go`: Legacy storage for routing trees\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/timeinterval/legacy_storage.go`: Legacy storage for time intervals\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/templategroup/legacy_storage.go`: Legacy storage for notification templates\\n\\n## Provisioning\\nThe provisioning system (`pkg/services/provisioning/`) handles alert rule configuration:\\n- `provisioning.go`: Orchestrates alerting provisioning including rule service, folder service, and receiver configuration\\n- `alerting/rules_provisioner.go`: Implements the provisioning logic for alert rules from configuration files\\n\\n## Configuration\\nUnified alerting configuration is defined in `pkg/setting/setting_unified_alerting.go` with `UnifiedAlertingSettings` struct that includes:\\n- AdminConfigPollInterval\\n- AlertmanagerConfigPollInterval\\n- DefaultConfiguration\\n- ExecuteAlerts\\n- BaseInterval\\n- RulesPerRuleGroupLimit\\n\\nThe migration system ensures that when users upgrade from legacy alerting to unified alerting, their alert rules and configurations are automatically converted while maintaining backward compatibility through legacy storage implementations.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
